Non-members may join NRA on-site to gain entry in to the Show.\n\n How does Exhibitor Move-In work?\n\n At the NRA Annual Meetings & Exhibits, there are two types of onsite move-in; traditional material handling, and POV.  Material Handling is the unloading of exhibit materials.  It includes delivery to your booth from the docks, handling of empty containers, and removal of materials from your booth for reloading onto your outbound carrier for a fee.  It is an essential service for many large exhibits and is provided by our general service contractor, GES. However, many of our smaller exhibitors may find this service expensive and unnecessary, especially when their material can fit in their own vehicle and be easily carried by hand! POV Move In is designed to allow smaller exhibitors to quickly and efficiently move in without competing with large commercial vehicles at the docks or incurring extraneous labor costs.  To qualify for POV Move In, you must be driving a vehicle weighing under one ton, (pickups, vans and SUVs all qualify,) and you must be able to empty your vehicle in 20 minutes.\n\n How do I update my online Directory Listing?\n\n [Click here](https://nraam2026.exh.mapyourshow.com/)https://nraam2024.exh.mapyourshow.com/to go to the Exhibitor Dashboard and enter your Exhibitor ID and Password.  Go to \"Directory Listing\"\n\nForgot your password? Go to the Exhibitor Dashboard link above and click \"Forgot Exhibitor ID or Password?\" and enter your primary contact email address to have it resent. If you need further assistance, email [[email protected]](/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)\n\n What if a non-official Contractor contacts me? Can I use them?\n\n Companies not selected by the NRA may reach out to you in order to solicit your business. This is happening most aggressively with housing companies. Please note that NRA Housing (ConferenceDirect[)](https://book.passkey.com/event/49903591/owner/6893/home) is our exclusive housing provider.   If you provide your credit card information to any other unauthorized vendors, your card may be charged, but you may not have a reservation when you arrive in Houston.\n\n What is Material Handling?\n\n Material Handling is the moving of materials from point A to point B. Whether your materials are sent in advance to the Service Contractor's warehouse or directly to Show site, they still need to get to your booth after the carrier drops them off. Paying for handling entitles you to have your freight brought to your booth from the loading dock, empty containers stored during the Show, empty containers returned to your booth at the close of the Show, and your freight carried back to the loading dock and loaded onto the carrier at the conclusion of the Show. Then you arrange for a carrier to pick up your exhibit materials for transport to the next destination. There is usually a 200 pound minimum per shipment charge for material handling. \n\n What can GES do for me?\n\n GES is our general service contractor and they can do it all! \n\n- Provide additional furnishings\n\n- Provide labor to assist move in or to erect your display\n\n- Track shipments\n\n- Verify order fulfillment\n\n- Answer questions regarding outbound bills of lading\n\n- Schedule outbound shipping through GES Logistics\n\n- Review order confirmations and billing\n\n- Remove empty crates (these should be labeled with an “EMPTY” sticker, found at the GES Service Desk as soon as they have been unpacked to keep the aisles clear and allow carpet installation.\n\nQuestions for GES? Please call them directly at 800-801-7648\n\n What is provided with my booth?\n\n Standard Booth Package:\nBooth Size: 10' x 10'\n8' High Backwall Drape: Red / White / Red\n3' High Sidewall Drape: Red\nAisle Carpet Color: Blue Jay\nPlease Note: The Facility is Not Carpeted.\n\n11\"x17\" Booth ID Sign\n\n How do I secure my firearms overnight at the Show?\n\n All firearms must be secured at night by either hiring overnight security, cabled and locked to the booth or taken to the Overnight Storage Room in a lockable storage room.\n\n I need extra meeting space during the show ... is that possible?\n\n Yes! We have meeting rooms for exhibitors to reserve at the George R. Brown Convention Center,  Marriott Marquis Houston, and Hilton Americas-Houston. - AB has AI assistant "AB Spotter" and AB Learn training tools
- **Hornady 4DOF**: Free app, no public API/licensing available
- **Kestrel**: Meters range $219-$992 with AB integration

**3. OEM Partnership Targets** (`memory/gundom-research/oem-partnership-targets.md`)
- **Vortex Optics**: Contact form (Marketing & Partnerships option), CEO Joe Hamilton, info@vortexoptics.com, 800-426-0048
- **Nightforce Optics**: marketing@nightforceoptics.com, (208) 476-9814, Orofino, ID
- **Leupold**: 1-800-LEUPOLD Option 4 for sales/partnerships, Beaverton, OR
- **Maven**: Direct-to-consumer model, Lander, WY; contact via mavenbuilt.com

**4. Gov/LE Procurement Paths** (`memory/gundom-research/gov-le-procurement-paths.md`)
- GSA Schedule 84: "Law Enforcement, Security, etc." - key vehicle for ballistics software
- State/local can access via Cooperative Purchasing Program
- SAM.gov shows Kestrel/Applied Ballistics already being procured (see: Tactical Equipment solicitations)
- GSA eOffer portal for becoming a GSA contractor
- Alternative: State contract vehicles (e.g., Pennsylvania eMarketplace)

### Key Insights for Gundom:
1. **NRA booth**: Budget $10K-25K+ for meaningful presence; sponsorship packages add significant visibility
2. **Applied Ballistics dominates** OEM partnerships (Kestrel, Garmin, SIG, Bushnell) - competitive moat
3. **Hornady 4DOF is free** - competitive threat for basic users, but no enterprise/API offering
4. **White-label opportunities**: Vortex and Maven are nimble/partnership-friendly; Nightforce and Leupold are more traditional
5. **Gov/LE path**: GSA Schedule 84 is the primary federal vehicle; requires formal application process
